           allowPrivilegeEscalation: false
+          readOnlyRootFilesystem: true
+          runAsNonRoot: true
       - name: prometheus-example-app
         image: quay.io/brancz/prometheus-example-app:v0.1.0
         args:
         - "--bind=127.0.0.1:8081"
+        resources:
+          limits:
+            cpu: 100m
+            memory: 200Mi
+          requests:
+            cpu: 100m
+            memory: 200Mi
+        securityContext:
+          readOnlyRootFilesystem: true
+          runAsNonRoot: true 
```
